 Babuji dhire chalna, pyar mein jara sambhalna Han bade dhokhe hain, bade dhokhe hain iss rah me Babuji dhire chalna......  Kyun ho khoye huye sar jhukaye, jaise jate ho sab kuchh lutaye Yeh toh babuji pehla kadam hai, najar aate hain apne paraye Han bade dhokhe hain, bade dhokhe hain iss rah me Babuji dhire chalna......  Yeh mohabbat hai o bholebhale, kar na dil ko gamo ke hawale Kam ulfat ka najuk bahut hai, aake hontho pe tutenge pyale Han bade dhokhe hain, bade dhokhe hain iss rah me Babuji dhire chalna......  Ho gayi hai kisi se jo anban, thamle dusra koyi daaman Jindagani ki rahein ajab hain, ho akela toh lakho hain dushman Han bade dhokhe hain, bade dhokhe hain iss rah me Babuji dhire chalna......
 Bachna ae hasino lo mai aa gaya Hay bachna ai hasino lo mai aa gaya Husn kaa aasheek, husn kaa dushman Apanee ada hai yaro se juda, hai ho Hai bachna.........  Hai duneeya me nahee hai, aaj meraa sa deevana Pyar valo kee juban pe, hai meraa hee tarana Sabkee rang bharee aankho pe aaj Chamak raha hai meraa hee nasha, hee ho Hai bachna..... Part 2:  Kahat kabir suno bhai sadho bat kahu mai kharee Yeh duniya ek nambaree toh mai das nambaree - (2)  Ek nanbar kaa hath dikhaya jab kah ke jay kalee Kitne hee setho kee bharee jebe ho gayee khalee Do nambar hai aur nirala dekhu aur khul jaye tala Udd ke jeb me aa jaye hare not kee paree Yeh duniya ek nambaree.......  Nambar tin kaa chamatkar dekho jab phenku patta Sabkee tabiyat karu saf dilli ho ya kalakatta Chauthe ne rah gajab kaa jhansa aap kiya dooje ko phansa Kabhee kabhee toh pulis ko ulte dikhalau hathakadee Yeh duniya ek nambaree.......  Panchava nambar julm kaa dushman mai dukhiyo kaa sathee Chhatha desh ke gaddaro sey chhin lu ghar kee batee Nambar sath kare jo danga ek hath me kar du changa Langadee tangadee chhuree kataree sab rah jaye dharee Yeh duniya ek nambaree.......  Kala aathavee yeh hai kee mai pyar sey milata sabse Pyar kee katir insan kya hai lad jau mai rab sey Navan jo mile mujhe hasina nau din tak naa ruke pasina Aur nambar das das Likha hai yeh toh har thane me sifat hai kya kya divane me Jitanee ungaliya inn hatho me utani jadugaree Yeh duniya ek nambaree.......
 Yeh hawa, yeh nadee kaa kinara Chand taro kaa rangin ishara Kah raha hain bekhabar, ho sake toh pyar kar Yeh sama milega phir naa dobara  Yeh rat dhalane naa paye, aane naa paye sawera Too bhee uthha lanbee palaken, julfo ko maine bikhera Yoonhee chanda tale meree naiyya chale, teree baho kaa leke sahara  Aise mile aaj saiyya, teree najar meree aankhe Dhadakan meree teraa dil ho, lab ho mere teree baten Dare kahe ko dil sajana khul ke mil kya karega jamana hamara Dare kahe ko dil goree aa khul ke mil kya karega jamana hamara
 Yeh kaun aaya roshan ho gayee mahafil kis ke naam se Mere ghar me jaise suraj nikala hain shaam se  Yaade hain kuchh aayee see, ya kirne laharaayee see Dil me soye gito ne lee hain phir angadaayee see Armaano kee madira chhalakee, aakhiyo ke jaam se  Aahat pe halakee halakee, chhatee dhadake paayal kee Har goree se naa musaka, yeh lahare puchhe aachal kee Chhupake chhupake radha koyee puchhe apane shaam se  Kya kahiye iss aane ko, aaya hain tarsane ko Dekha usane has has ke, har apane begaane ko Lekin kitna beparwa hai, mere hee salaam se
 Naa jane kyu naa jane kyu Yeh khushee kee mehafil dhadakta hai dil naa jane kyon Inn hajaro me sanam tumhi ko diya dil naa jane kyon Tumhe chah ke mere hasin kuchh aur phir chaha nahee Hal yeh huwa jane kyon, yeh khushee kee mehfil ...  Jee me jo aaye karo itna magar dekh lo Hathon me hai jo hath vahi arman kaa katil naa ho Hay alla teree najar jakhmee hai meraa jigar Katil dil ke mere kahee too hee meraa dil naa ho Ho teraa shabab khilata rahe jadu teraa chalta rahe Hain duwa meree jane kyon, inn hajaro me........  Mehafil ko roshan karo kuchh aur bhee rang bharo Aaisa bandho saman koyee hosh me naa rahe Darta hu iss pyar par kal ko hansee naa yeh log Do pal kee yeh khushee ban jaye jivan kaa rog Abb toh sanam chaha tumhe abb log jo chahe kahe Dil diya toh phir darna kyon, yeh khushee kee mehfil........
 (Yeh ladka hai allah kaisa hai divana Kitna mushkil hai tauba isko samjhana Ke dhire dhire dil bekarar hota hai Hote hote hote, pyar hota hai) - (2) Ho yeh ladka hai allah kaisa hai divana  (Hamne toh itna dekha, hamne toh itna sikha Dil kaa sauda hota hai, sauda jindagee kaa) - (2) Milte hee kaise koyee hota hai divana Kitna mushkil hai tauba isko samjhana Ke dhire dhire dil bekarar hota hai Hote hote hote, pyar hota hai Ho yeh ladka hai allah kaisa hai divana  (Ho sakta hai dekho naa, samjho mittee ko sona Pal bhar kaa hasna ho jaye jivan bhar kaa rona) - (2) Dekho jaldee me kabhee dil ko naa lagana Kitna mushkil hai tauba isko samjhana Ke dhire dhire dil bekarar hota hai Hote hote hote, pyar hota hai Oh yeh ladka hai allah kaisa hai divana  (Bholee ho tum kya jano, abhee mujhko pehchano Sapna tumhara mai hu, mano ya naa mano) - (2) Dekho nadanee se mujhe naa thukrana Nahee toh gatee hir hogee yeh tarana Ke dhire dhire dil bekarar hota hai Hote hote hote, pyar hota hai
 (Yeh mastaani dagar matwaali waadiya Baahon ko thaamati rangili daaliya Aisa sama milata hai re kahaan Haay re mujhako ai dil abb toh gum ho jaane de yahaan) - (2)  Sang mere jhule tan meera chume Resham jaisa bheega bheega udate baadal ka dhunwaan Yeh mastaani dagar matwaali waadiya Baahon ko thaamati rangili daaliya Aisa sama milata hai re kahaan Haay re mujhako ai dil abb toh gum ho jaane de yahaan  Jab hawa laage dil mera jaage, akhiya dole kaliya bole Meri dhadkan ki jubaan Yeh mastaani dagar matwaali waadiya Baahon ko thaamati rangili daaliya Aisa sama milata hai re kahaan Haay re mujhako ai dil abb toh gum ho jaane de yahaan
 Yeh mera jivan tere liye hai, jivan kaa sapna tere liye hai Mang le hans ke kya chahiye tujhe, meri toh duniya tere liye hai Yeh mera jivan tere liye........  Dali pe baithi chhoti si chidiya Kandhe pe mere nanhi si gudiya Chidiya se bhi sundar meri gudiya Yeh mera jivan tere liye........  Dekha tha sapna jo jindagi kaa Yeh bhi toh waisa hi din hai kushi kaa Jine kaa dhang tujhse maine sikha Yeh mera jivan tere liye........  Mano badal jaye dono ki manjil Phir bhi rahega sath mera dil Chahenge toh milana nahi mushkil Yeh mera jivan tere liye........
 Yeh mera jiwan tere liye hai Jiwan kaa sapna tere liye hai Mang le hasake kya chahiye tujhe Meri toh dooniya tere liye hai  Dali pe baithi chhoti si chidiya Kandhe pe mere nanhi si gudiya Chidiya se bhi sundar meri gudiya Yeh mera jiwan.........  Dekha tha sapna jo jindgi kaa Yeh bhi toh waisa hee din hai khushi kaa Jine kaa dhang tujhse maine sikha Yeh mera jiwan.........  Mano badal jayey dono kee manjil Phir bhi rahega sath mera dil Chahenge toh milana nahee mushkil Yeh mera jiwan.........

 Yeh rate yeh mausam nadee ka kinara, yeh chanchal hawa - (2) Kaha do dilo ne ke milkar kabhee ham na honge juda Yeh rate yeh mausam nadee ka kinara, yeh chanchal hawa  Yeh kya bat hai, aaj kee chandnee me - (2) Ke ham kho gaye, pyar kee raganee me Yeh baho me bahe, yeh behkee nigahe Lo aane laga jindagee ka maja Yeh rate yeh mausam nadee ka kinara, yeh chanchal hawa  Sitaro kee mehfil ne karke ishara - (2) Kaha abb toh sara jahan hai tumhara Mohabbat jawan ho, khula aasman ho Kare koyee dil aarju aur kya Yeh rate yeh mausam nadee ka kinara, yeh chanchal hawa  Kasam hai tumhe, tum agar mujhse ruthe - (2) Rahe sans jab tak yeh bandhan na tute Tumhe dil diya hai, yeh wada kiya hai Sanam mai tumharee rahungee sada Yeh rate yeh mausam nadee ka kinara, yeh chanchal hawa Kaha do dilo ne, ke milkar kabhee ham na honge juda Yeh rate yeh mausam nadee ka kinara, yeh chanchal hawa
 Aa aa........ Jo bhee mere dil pe bita pyaar kee baajee mai hee jita Re yeh toh hona hee tha, koyee chaahe naa chaahe Yeh toh hona hee tha.......  Har galee ko saja do, raat ko jagamaga do Aaj har sundaree ko balam sang nacha do Har ek dafalee ke sang jame paayal ke rang Chhalake pyaale khushee ke, ho chhalake pyaale khushee ke Yeh toh hona hee tha.......  Meraa yeh jo jahan hai Meraa yeh kal bhee tha, aaj bhee yahee meraa Sapane saja mere dil, meree bhigee palak pe naa jaa Rahe itanee khabar nayan chhalake agar Chhalake aansu khushee ke, ho chhalake aansu khushee ke Yeh toh hona hee tha.......  Jindagee kaa thikaana Tune ha kar dee jaanee, jee utha mai divaana Mujhe toh jab se yaar mila hai teraa pyaar Jhumata hu khushee se, ho jhumata hu khushee se Yeh toh hona hee tha.......

 Zamane ne mare javan kaise kaise - 2 Zami kha gai aasman kaise kaise Zamane ne mare javan kaise kaise  (Pale the jo kal rang me phul me Kahi kho gaye raah ki dhul mai) - (2) Hue darbadar karvan kaise kaise Zamane ne mare javan kaise kaise Zami kha gai aasman kaise kaise Zamane ne mare javan kaise kaise  (Hazaro ke tan kaise shishe ho chur Jala dhup me kitni aankho ka nur) - (2) Hy chehre pe gam ke nishan kaise kaise Zamane ne mare javan kaise kaise Zami kha gai aasman kaise kaise Zamane ne mare javan kaise kaise  Lahu ban ke bahate vo aansu tamam Ki hoga inhi se baharo ka naam Banege abhi aashiya kaise kaise Zamane ne mare javan kaise kaise
 Zindagi ko jab hamaara ghum nahi Hamako ki bhi kyun jindagi ka ghum rahe Are dum lage jab tak ke dum mein dum rahe, dum rahe, dum rahe Zindagi ko jab hamaara ghum nahi  Bas yeh pal hai tere paas bhul ja aage ki baat Isake aage jo bhi hai dhoka hai Aaj hi hai jindagi aaj hi hai maut bhi Kal kahaan hai kal kisane dekha hai Dum lage jab tak ke dum mein dum rahe, dum rahe, dum rahe Zindagi ko jab hamaara ghum nahi Hamako ki bhi kyun jindagi ka ghum rahe Are dum lage jab tak ke dum mein dum rahe, dum rahe, dum rahe Zindagi ko jab hamaara ghum nahi  Chaah kya kuchh bhi nahi, pyaar kya kuchh bhi nahi Ek naadaani hai naadaano ki Dushamani bhi jhut hai dosti bhi jhut hai Jhut saari baatein insaano ki Dum lage jab tak ke dum mein dum rahe, dum rahe, dum rahe Zindagi ko jab hamaara ghum nahi Hamako ki bhi kyun jindagi ka ghum rahe Are dum lage jab tak ke dum mein dum rahe, dum rahe, dum rahe Zindagi ko jab hamaara ghum nahi
